<Rating>5</Rating>< Review>
I was in at the same time as reviewer John Munoz (Villanueva). We walked in at the same exact time on Valentine's Day morning, yesterday. This florist is very busy for good reason. Luis, half of the husband-wife duo running the show, explained that on Valentine's Day, walk-in orders are not feasible unless you are willing to wait. He reasoned that there were over a hundred orders ahead of us and it would not be fair to everyone who already ordered and paid weeks or even months in advance. This guy was not happy with this info and stormed off in a big huff. How can you review a business if you haven't even been a customer before? I know they would never turn away a potential customer on any other day. His review, which fails to mention critical details, should not even be posted up as it is in no way accurate for this business.

Anyway, I was happy to wait. There is a reason Darling's Holm & Olson is so busy. Aida always has the best arrangement designs and freshest flowers, and the locals (and plenty not-so-local) know it. My family and friends have been customers for at least 20 years and probably more. Hands down this is the only florist worth visiting in Los Angeles. Any other day I know I can expect to walk in here and within 15 minutes, have the most fragrant, freshest flowers filling my car with their enticing aroma. I don't know how anyone could give this place less than 5 stars!< /Review>

< Review>
Can't rate the balloon. Didn't ride it. However our tour guide Amy was great. As well as the other staff members. Part of our party was late getting there but the other guide made sure we met up during our tour. Oh and don't get the nachos the cheese is cold.</Review>
</record>
</dataset><record>
< text>
This ride is very gentle and goes up to 400 ft in the air. This is a great ride for the whole family as any age can ride on the Balloon. If they are 12 or older they can ride alone, as long as the waiver is filled out by an adult. Under 12 years old a parent must accompany the child. The employees are very kind and helpful. It's tethered by a cable going up and down like an elevator. It does sway a little if there's some breezy wind passing through but it's calm. It's filled with helium, yes helium like a regular balloon would be. It's also wheelchair accessible if your wheelchair fits the gondola doors. If it doesn't fit they do have thier own wheelchair in which one can transfer into. Once in the air you can see the whole park and animals you don't normally see on the tram. Also depending on your membership level you may get a discount.< /text>

<Text>Edit: Subtracting one star  ‚ûñ‚≠êüí®; the last pizza I got was very skimpy on the sundried tomatoes (yet had at least 5x as many fresh tomatoes üçÖ) and I found a small, sharp piece of what is presumably üçóCHICKEN BONE üçñ Luckily, I tend to eat mindfully/carefully and was able to pull it out once I noticed. Original review: At first I thought the sesame seed crust was a little strange (one can't argue it's certainly unique!), but this place is starting to grow on me. This space has changed ownership several times over the past 30 years but it's always been a small pizza place. If you're old enough, you might remember when it was Little Caesars. More recently, it was "Triple Seven Pizzeria" or 777 Pizzaria, which offered by-the-slice lunch specials. Since it reincarnated into Stacker's, they don't do slices anymore, though you can get an 8" personal pan pizza for $8. There's only enough room for a few tables inside, so this is the kind of place you go for take-out (or delivery if you meet the $18 minimum), or maybe a quick lunch if you call ahead or use their website to order. Although the one time we tried ordering through their website, it didn't work :/ So far I've tried the combination and pesto chicken pizzas. Both were good. The sesame-seed coated crust they do standard on all their pizzas is very unique. The crust on the pesto pizza also had a very buttery taste, which is a good sign. They offer whole wheat in addition to regular white refined flour crust! They also offer soda in 2-liter size, cans, or 6-packs.< /Text>< Response>

< text>
Found out this new restaurant on google maps because their cute walls! This restaurant actually in the food court, it was a little bit hard to find at the beginning. We ordered wagyu beef sukiyaki don with tofu and mushrooms in side this dish. The guy helped us was really nice and have friendly customer service. They have chair outside this food court, and with their hot soup, we had an amazing night. Perfect food for winter. Very delicious food, if we in this area again, will definitely come back! Highly recommended!</text>
